tbm_grant_air_cas_endsieg = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_endsieg value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
            check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1918 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            has_country_flag = tbm_cat_cas
            check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            check_variable = { var = tbm_air_competence value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_endsieg value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1918 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            tbm_grant_air_cas_y1918_endsieg = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_endsieg value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1922 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            tbm_grant_air_cas_y1922_endsieg = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_endsieg value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1925 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            tbm_grant_air_cas_y1925_endsieg = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_endsieg value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1936 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            tbm_grant_air_cas_y1936_endsieg = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_endsieg value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1940 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            tbm_grant_air_cas_y1940_endsieg = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_endsieg value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1944 compare = greater_than_or_equals }

tbm_grant_air_cas_y1918_endsieg = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_endsieg value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
            check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1918 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            has_country_flag = tbm_cat_cas
            check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            check_variable = { var = tbm_air_competence value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            NOT = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone" }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { has_tech = early_CAS }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_endsieg value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1918 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_air_competence value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                has_country_flag = tbm_cat_cas
                NOT = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone" }
            }
            set_technology = { early_CAS = 1 popup = no }
            add_to_variable = { tbm_grant_counter_endsieg = 1 }
            tbm_handle_tech_grant_notification = yes
        }
    }
}

        limit = {
            check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_endsieg value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
            check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_industry value = 1959 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            has_country_flag = tbm_cat_rockets
            check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 5 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            check_variable = { var = tbm_industry_competence value = 85 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            tbm_advanced_tech_allowed = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { has_tech = nuke_rocket_engines }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_endsieg value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_industry value = 1959 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 5 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_industry_competence value = 85 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                has_country_flag = tbm_cat_rockets
                tbm_advanced_tech_allowed = yes
            }
            set_technology = { nuke_rocket_engines = 1 popup = no }
            add_to_variable = { tbm_grant_counter_endsieg = 1 }
            tbm_handle_tech_grant_notification = yes
        }
    }
}
